msg:The address of Wuhan Shangri-La is excellent. I have to sigh at the geographical location of Shangri-La Group. It is quiet in the bustling area, backed by Vientiane City, and a taxi starting price away from the bustling Wansongyuan. There is also a Hong Kong Road Station where many subway lines intersect. It can be said that it is very convenient to travel whether you choose to take a taxi or the subway.
Before checking in, I communicated with the front desk duty manager, Mr. Zhou, about my needs. After learning that I was traveling alone, he was very straightforward and polite to prepare the room for me in advance and make corresponding notes of my preferences.
The hotel's Deluxe Pavilion is located on the 20th floor. Mr. Tony Hu, the manager of the lounge, is very gentle every time we meet. After learning about some of my needs, he is also very nice to take me to visit other rooms and provide me with room changes, which makes me feel very relieved and grateful. Of course, under his leadership, the staff of the Deluxe Pavilion Lounge, whether Jean/Fei Yan/Nick, are very warm and polite, and they are very smart and thoughtful in handling things. Thank you Ms. Jean for paying special attention to my food taboos during my stay and arranging my breakfast thoughtfully. When I checked out, Fei Yan gave me a cute little gift that surprised me. During my stay, the experience brought to me by the Horizon Club was extraordinary. The snacks and drinks provided all day long during the day were really attentive, and the breakfast muffins were really delicious, just as worthy of praise as their attentive service.
After talking about accommodation and food, let's talk about travel. This time I chose Wuhan and I left on a whim, and I booked the air tickets and hotels temporarily. So I don't know much about Wuhan. I was very happy that the sunny Tim from the concierge department answered me and explained the map of Wuhan travel and the surrounding subway line arrangements. This saved me a lot of detours and I went to many fun places. He also asked me to pay attention to sun protection, which was really considerate! Secondly, I would like to thank Mr. Vincent Liao very much. I am very happy to chat with him every time. The weather in Wuhan is very changeable. Thank you for providing me with an umbrella and remembering my preferences very carefully. He also reminded me not to get cold, so I have a good impression of him! Finally, I am very grateful to him for helping me with my luggage when I left the hotel. He is always very good and kind, and I am really satisfied.
The hotel's decoration design is very classical and old-fashioned. Although the facilities and equipment cannot be compared with the latest hotels, the service of Shangri-La will always rank first in my mind. Finally, I would like to thank Sister Feirong and Manager Zhu Min from the Housekeeping Department for helping to take care of my room. Thank you for your meticulous service and for cleaning my room meticulously~
In short, I still love Shangri-La 
Finally, I would like to thank Louis, the most enthusiastic and friendly person who provided me with meticulous service during my stay/ Allen, the calm and thoughtful Paul. Thank you for providing me with the warmth of a home away from home 
Wuhan, see you next time~

Later, I paid special attention to the external price of the buffet and finally decided to stay in Wuhan Shangri-La. The hotel is elegantly beige, neither old-fashioned nor out of place. After many years, it is still comfortable and pleasing to the eye. The lobby, guest rooms, fitness center, swimming pool facilities and water temperature are full of international style, especially the buffet breakfast, Western butter, jam, bread, bacon, sausage, curry beef, borscht, etc. Japanese natto sushi, Chinese porridge, noodles, vegetable salad, various fungi and vegetables are especially friendly to slightly picky foodies. The transportation is very convenient, and you can transfer at Exit A of Hong Kong Road Subway Station. There are no blind spots in the service throughout the whole process, from delivering water to the guest room to communicating with the fitness coach, from the provision of preserved egg and lean meat porridge with ginger to mustard, the response is fast, there is no selective amnesia service status, and the unexcessive requirements are easily met.
